## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    Git[GitLab Repository] -->|Clone| ArgoCD[ArgoCD Controller]
    ArgoCD -->|Read Helm Charts| Helm[Helm Templates]
    Helm -->|Apply Values| Config[Merged Configuration]
    Config -->|Deploy| K8s[Kubernetes Cluster]
    K8s -->|Monitor| CW[Amazon CloudWatch]
    ArgoCD -->|Auto Sync| K8s
    K8s -->|Drift Detected| ArgoCD
    ArgoCD -->|Self Heal| K8s
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Application {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +Spec spec
    }
    class Metadata {
        +String name
        +Map labels
    }
    class Spec {
        +Destination destination
        +Source source
        +String project
        +SyncPolicy syncPolicy
    }
    class Destination {
        +String name
        +String namespace
        +String server
    }
    class Source {
        +String path
        +String repoURL
        +String targetRevision
        +Helm helm
    }
    class Helm {
        +List valueFiles
        +List parameters
    }
    class SyncPolicy {
        +Automated automated
        +List syncOptions
    }
    class Automated {
        +Boolean prune
        +Boolean selfHeal
    }
    
    Application --> Metadata
    Application --> Spec
    Spec --> Destination
    Spec --> Source
    Spec --> SyncPolicy
    Source --> Helm
    SyncPolicy --> Automated
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> OutOfSync: Application Created
    OutOfSync --> Syncing: Automated Sync Triggered
    Syncing --> Healthy: Deployment Successful
    Healthy --> OutOfSync: Configuration Drift Detected
    Healthy --> Degraded: Health Check Failed
    Degraded --> Syncing: Self Heal Triggered
    Syncing --> Failed: Deployment Failed
    Failed --> Syncing: Retry
    Healthy --> [*]: Application Deleted
```
